<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="External_links">External links</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Poverty&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: External links">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1097025294">.mw-parser-output .side-box{margin:4px 0;box-sizing:border-box;border:1px solid #aaa;font-size:88%;line-height:1.25em;background-color:#f9f9f9}.mw-parser-output .side-box-abovebelow,.mw-parser-output .side-box-text{padding:0.25em 0.9em}.mw-parser-output .side-box-image{padding:2px 0 2px 0.9em;text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .side-box-imageright{padding:2px 0.9em 2px 0;text-align:center}@media(min-width:500px){.mw-parser-output .side-box-flex{display:flex;align-items:center}.mw-parser-output .side-box-text{flex:1}}@media(min-width:720px){.mw-parser-output .side-box{width:238px}.mw-parser-output .side-box-right{clear:right;float:right;margin-left:1em}.mw-parser-output .side-box-left{margin-right:1em}}</style><div class="side-box side-box-right plainlinks sistersitebox">

<div class="side-box-text plainlist">Wikiquote has quotations related to <i><b><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikiquote.org/wiki/Special:Search/Poverty" title="q:Special:Search/Poverty">Poverty</a></b></i>.</div></div>

<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1097025294" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="side-box side-box-right plainlinks sistersitebox">
<div class="side-box-flex">
<div class="side-box-image"><img alt="" class="noviewer" data-file-height="512" data-file-width="626" decoding="async" height="33" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Wikiversity_logo_2017.svg/40px-Wikiversity_logo_2017.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Wikiversity_logo_2017.svg/60px-Wikiversity_logo_2017.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Wikiversity_logo_2017.svg/80px-Wikiversity_logo_2017.svg.png 2x" width="40"/></div>
<div class="side-box-text plainlist">Wikiversity has learning resources about <i><b><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikiversity.org/wiki/Eliminating_poverty" title="v:Eliminating poverty">Eliminating poverty</a></b></i></div></div>
</div>
<ul><li><a class="external text" href="https://repository.library.georgetown.edu/handle/10822/552568" rel="nofollow">Addressing Global Poverty</a> from the <a class="external text" href="https://repository.library.georgetown.edu/handle/10822/552494" rel="nofollow">Dean Peter Krogh Foreign Affairs Digital Archives</a></li>
<li><a class="external text" href="https://ourworldindata.org/extreme-poverty" rel="nofollow">Data visualizations of the long-run development of poverty and list of data sources on poverty</a> on 'Our World in Data'.</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20090918223238/http://www.isdb.org/irj/portal/anonymous" rel="nofollow">Islamic Development Bank</a></li>
<li><a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20051204101908/http://www.lisproject.org/" rel="nofollow">Luxembourg Income Study</a> Contains a wealth of data on income inequality and poverty, and hundreds of its sponsored research papers using this data.</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://www.oecd.org/" rel="nofollow">Organization for Economic Cooperation and Development</a> Contains reports on economic development as well as relations between rich and poor nations.</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="https://ophi.org.uk/" rel="nofollow">OPHI</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Oxford_Poverty_%26_Human_Development_Initiative" title="Oxford Poverty &amp; Human Development Initiative">Oxford Poverty &amp; Human Development Initiative</a> (OPHI) Research to advance the human development approach to poverty reduction.</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://www.transparency.org/" rel="nofollow">Transparency International</a> Tracks issues of government and corporate corruption around the world.</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="https://www.un.org/" rel="nofollow">United Nations</a> Hundreds of free reports related to economic development and standards of living in countries around the world, such as the annual <i>Human Development Report.</i></li>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://www.usaid.gov/" rel="nofollow">US Agency for International Development</a> USAID is the primary US government agency with the mission for aid to developing countries.</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://www.worldbank.org/" rel="nofollow">World Bank</a> Contains hundreds of reports which can be downloaded for free, such as the annual <i>World Development Report.</i></li>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://www.wfp.org/" rel="nofollow">World Food Program</a> Associated with the United Nations, the World Food Program compiles hundreds of reports on hunger and food security around the world.</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://www.whypoverty.net/" rel="nofollow">Why poverty</a> Documentary films about poverty broadcast on television around the world in November 2012, then will be available online.</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="https://www.oxfam.org/en/press-releases/annual-income-richest-100-people-enough-end-global-poverty-four-times-over" rel="nofollow">Annual income of richest 100 people enough to end global poverty four times over</a>. <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Oxfam_International" title="Oxfam International">Oxfam International</a>,</i> 19 January 2013.</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=xxZi6pe2DgQC&amp;pg=PA15&amp;dq=poverty+belgium+1975&amp;hl=en&amp;sa=X&amp;ei=Z3-dU8DKD8G-O8XugcgH&amp;ved=0CCkQ6AEwAg#v=onepage&amp;q=poverty%20belgium%201975&amp;f=false" rel="nofollow">Contains estimates on the number of people living in poverty in selected countries from 1973 to 1985</a></li>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://hdr.undp.org/sites/default/files/hdr14-summary-en.pdf" rel="nofollow">Summary of Human Development Report 2014</a>, by the <i><a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Development_Programme" title="United Nations Development Programme">United Nations Development Programme</a></i></li>
<li><a class="external text" href="https://www.jacobinmag.com/2014/11/making-poverty-history/" rel="nofollow">Making Poverty History</a>, by <a href="/wiki/Vijay_Prashad" title="Vijay Prashad">Vijay Prashad</a> for <i><a href="/wiki/Jacobin_(magazine)" title="Jacobin (magazine)">Jacobin</a>.</i> 10 November 2014.</li></ul>
